 Incidents of car fires are becoming common these days
 kuch saal pehle tata kii naino main aag lag jane kii khabaren kuch zyada hi aane lagi thim to vahiin lagjri car porsh 911 GT3 main bhi aag lag jane kii khabaren bhi sunne ko mili thim
 However, the companies of these cars took immediate action and removed their technical flaws
 lekin zyaadaatar maamalon main company kii galatiyon kii vajah se nahin balki car chaalak kii laaparvaahee kii vajah se aisi ghatnaayen ho jaati hai
 We are telling you what may be the reasons for the fire in the car and what measures can you take to avoid such cases
 car main aag lagane kii vajah1
 Most people buy and fit accessories such as car stereos, security systems, head lamps and reverse parking sensors from outside shops after purchasing a car
 aise maamalon main dekha gaya he ki aprashikshit mechainic fitting karte vakt kai taron ko khulaa chhod dete hai yaa taron ko sahi tareeke se nahin jodate
 This is a major reason for short circuit
 2
 In most of the cases, it is seen that after the purchase of the car, after the free servicing given by the company is over, people get their car serviced by an external mechanic
 aise main aprishikshit maikenic kai baar laaparvaahee kar jate hai or phir aisi ghatnaon kaa saamana karnaa padataa he
 3
 aaj kii taarikh main har car nirmaataa company phitted sienji / alpiji kit uplabdh nahin karaata
 In such cases, people get CNG / LPG kits fitted by unauthorized dealers
 aise main kai baar silinder main likege kii samasyaon kaa saamana karnaa padataa he jo aag lagane kii ek badi vajah he
 What is rescue 1
 car kii ingine kaa khaas dhyaan dene kii jarurat he
 For example, keep changing the oil filter, engine coolant and engine oil at the right time
 isse car kii health thik rahegi
 2
 car main phaltu ke electrical upkaran lagane se bachein
 These add extra load to your car's battery
 3
 Take and fit the CNG / LPG kit from the usual authorized center
 4
 Avoid over-modification in the car
 isse car main takneekee kharabi aane kii sambhaavna bad jaati he
 What happens when a car is on fire 1
 aag lagane ke baad sabase pehle car ke power windos, seat belt or central loking system fail ho jate hai
 Which may require a lot of effort to get out of the car
 2
 If the information about the fire is not received in time, due to carbon monoxide, people sitting in the car can die
 car main rakhen ye jaruri saamaan1
 Hammer: This will help you break the glass of the car
 2
 Scissors: If the seat belt is locked, with the help of scissors you can cut it
 3
 Firefighting: a small firefighter can help you in the event of a fire
 isaki madad se aap aag par kaabo paa sakate hai
 If your car catches fire, never try to extinguish it with water, this increases the chances of short circuit

 a new research at the University of Copenhagen, Denmark, suggested several times to think before the use of paracetamol

 In this, research on animals has found the use of the popular analgesic paracetamol to be harmful for the development of male behavior
 shodhakartaaon ne kaha he ki chuuhe ko di gai khuraaq ek garbhvatee mahila ko di jane vaali khuraaq ke lagbhag baraabar rahi

 shodh ke dauraan copenhegan vishvavidhyalay se jude rahe david mobajarg critensen ne kaha ki shodhakartaaon dwaara paracetamol ke hanikaarak prabhaav kii nischitata kii vajah se iskaa pareekshan maanav par kiya janaa anuchit hoga
 Möbjerg Kritensen, associated with the Environment at Trouvel (IRSET) in France and now the Institut de Richerche in Sante, said, "in a trial, rats given paracetamol were simply unable to orgasm like the rats we controlled
 bhrun ke vikaas ke dauraan inamen purush pranali kaa vikaas sahi dhang se nahin hua or yah unke baad ke vayask jivan kaal main bhi dekha ja saktaa he

 "tippaniyan Mozberg Christensen stated that earlier research has found that the use of paracetamol inhibits the growth of testosterone sex hormones in male fetuses
